***могущество.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:могущество.html>могу́щество</a> (10057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́щий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mogúščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ество</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-estvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:могущество.html>могу́щество</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mogúščestvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:могущество.html>могу́щества</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:могущество.html>могу́щества</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:могущество.html>могу́ществ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>might, power</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:моделировать.html>модели́ровать</a> (26211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модель.html>моде́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">modɛ́lʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моделировать.html>модели́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">modɛlírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:моделировать.html>модели́ровать</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смоделировать.html>смодели́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to model, to design, to fashion, to shape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to simulate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">art</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to model, to sculpture</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:модерн.html>моде́рн</a> (21239)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">moderne</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модерн.html>моде́рн</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">modɛ́rn</span>) (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> modern, contemporary, fashionable</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Normally used either in the post-position or as a predicative adjective.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">модерно́вый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">modɛrnóvyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fashionable, contemporary (colloquial)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модерн.html>моде́рн</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">modɛ́rn</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:модернизировать.html>модернизи́ровавший</a> (31542)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:модница.html>мо́дница</a> (23265)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мода.html>мо́д</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́к</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mód(nik)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модница.html>мо́дница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">módnica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модница.html>мо́дницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модница.html>мо́дницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модница.html>мо́дниц</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мо́дник</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> female fashionista, fashionable woman</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:модуль.html>мо́дуль</a> (14275)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">modulus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модуль.html>мо́дуль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">módulʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модуль.html>мо́дуля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модуль.html>мо́дули</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:модуль.html>мо́дулей</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мо́дульный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">general<span class="ib-comma">,</span> architecture<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> etc.</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> module</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> absolute value, modulus <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">non-negative, real-valued magnitude of a real or complex number</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> modulus <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">coefficient expressing how much of a certain property is possessed by a certain substance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***можно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a> (103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мог-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mog-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (but the form **<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мо́жный</span> does not exist).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">móžno</span>) (<i>impersonal, invariable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>one can, one may
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>móžno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I may</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>it is possible
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a></b> лу́чше</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>móžno</b> lúčše</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the best way possible</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a> скоре́е</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak móžno skoréje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">as soon as possible</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мочь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">močʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The forms "**<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">немо́жно</span>" or "**<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a></span>" are not used in standard Russian. To negate <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a></span>, use <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nelʹzjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which doesn't have a positive form "<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">льзя</span>", or <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможно.html>возмо́жно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ne vozmóžno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

***мозг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозг</a> (970)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mozgъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mozg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мо́зга</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозго́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> brain; marrow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головной.html>головно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">golovnój mozg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cerebrum</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинной.html>спинно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мо́зг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">spinnój mózg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">spinal cord</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:костный.html>ко́стный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kóstnyj mozg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bone marrow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продолговатый.html>продолгова́тый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prodolgovátyj mozg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">medulla oblongata</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> brains (usually as food)</li></ol>

***мозоль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозоль.html>мозо́ль</a> (11772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозоль.html>мозо́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mozólʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозоль.html>мозо́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозоль.html>мозо́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мозоль.html>мозо́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>callus, corn</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***мой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> (55)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mojь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">moj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">possessive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> my, mine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">«<b><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:москва.html>москва́</a>»</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">“<b>Mojá</b> Moskvá”</i> ― <span class="e-translation">"<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moya_Moskva" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Moya Moskva"><b>My</b> Moscow</a>"</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́йка</a> (13962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мойка.html>мо́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>washing</li>
<li>sink (basin), kitchen sink</li>
<li>washer</li></ol>

***мокнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мокнуть.html>мо́кнуть</a> (15242)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мокнути</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">moknuti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*moknǫti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to become/get wet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокнуть.html>мо́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">móknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to get wet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мокнуть.html>мо́кнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>móknutʹ</b> pod doždjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be out in the rain</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to soak</li></ol>

***мокрица.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мокрица.html>мокри́ца</a> (32374)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрый.html>мо́крый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mókryj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ца</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрица.html>мокри́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mokríca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрица.html>мокри́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрица.html>мокри́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрица.html>мокри́ц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>woodlouse, sowbug <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">any species of suborder Oniscidea</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>common chickweed (<i>Stellaria media</i>)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">звездча́тка <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дняя</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zvezdčátka srédnjaja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mokrъ</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрый.html>мо́крый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mókryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мокре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мокре́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wet, damp</li>
